Oct 15, 2025 • 372 min read

wip   braxen 

!cat /tmp/braxen-eng.txt |awk -F'\t' '{print $2}'|tr ' ' '\n'|sort|uniq -c |sort -nr > /tmp/braxen-eng.freq

!tail -n 8 /tmp/braxen-eng.freq|awk '{print $2}'|while read i;do echo $i; grep " $i " /tmp/braxen-eng.txt || grep "$i " /tmp/braxen-eng.txt;echo;done
